## GT Analysis

The GT expression is:
```

```

```

Computing: 0.05077*278.15 ≈ 14.12, so (-0.05077*T + 14.12 + 1) = (-0.05077*T + 15.12)

First term: 61.35*epsilon*(-0.05077*T + 15.12) = -3.114*T*epsilon + 927.6*epsilon

So GT = -3.114*T*epsilon + 927.6*epsilon + 98.58*epsilon^0.3178*exp(-5.949/T) + 2.304*T*epsilon^1.450 - 640.9*epsilon^1.450

The GT has these basis function components:
1. **T*epsilon** (linear in both)
2. **epsilon** (linear)
3. **epsilon^0.3178 * exp(-5.949/T)** (fractional power of epsilon times Arrhenius in T)
4. **T * epsilon^1.450** (T times fractional power of epsilon)
5. **epsilon^1.450** (fractional power of epsilon)

The critical feature is the **exp(-c/T)** Arrhenius term. This cannot be replicated by any polynomial, logarithmic, or exp(c*epsilon) type terms.

```
